<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The First-Quarter 2023 Earnings Release furnished as Exhibit 99 hereto, which is incorporated by reference into this Item 2.02, was posted on the SLB internet website (<span style="text-decoration:underline">https://investorcenter.slb.com/financials/quarterly-results</span>) on April&#160;21, 2023. In accordance with General Instructions B.2. of Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> the information will not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), nor will it be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the &#8220;Securities Act&#8221;), except as expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;7.01</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Regulation FD Disclosure. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">On April&#160;21, 2023, SLB issued a press release, a copy of which is furnished with this <span style="white-space:nowrap">Form&#160;8-K</span> as Exhibit&#160;99 and incorporated into this Item 7.01 by reference. In accordance with General Instruction B.2. of Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> the information will not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Exchange Act, nor will it be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act, except as expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Also, see Item 2.02, &#8220;Results of Operations and Financial Condition.&#8221; </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">n/m = not meaningful </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Strong Growth and
Broad-Based Attributes </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">SLB CEO Olivier Le Peuch commented,&nbsp;&#147;I am very pleased with our start to 2023. We delivered strong year-over-year revenue
growth and margin expansion at a scale that instills further confidence in our full-year financial ambition. The quarter was defined by strong activity dynamics offshore and in the broader international basins, most notably in Well Construction and
Production Systems. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Compared to the same period last year, revenue grew 30%; adjusted EBITDA increased 43%; EPS&#151;excluding charges and
credits&#151;increased 85%; and pretax segment operating margin expanded 298 basis points (bps). All Divisions grew, both in North America and in the international markets, reflecting the strength of our portfolio across geographies and business
lines. Revenue growth surpassed rig count growth both in North America and internationally&#151;representing the highest <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> quarterly growth in more than a
decade. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Sequentially, revenue grew 4% in North America, our eighth consecutive quarter of growth, benefiting from our exposure to the most resilient basins
and market segments. Internationally, the sequential revenue decline was less pronounced than historical trends as seasonal effects were partially offset by robust activity gains.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;We continue to see positive pricing as our performance differentiates, technology adoption increases, contract terms are adjusted to offset inflation, and service
capacity continues to tighten in key international markets. In this environment, our customers are more actively collaborating with us to improve their operational performance, attain decarbonization objectives, and lower overall costs through the
increased use of our differentiated technologies. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;First-quarter cash flow from operations was $330&nbsp;million, reflecting the seasonal first-quarter buildup of
working capital that will support our anticipated growth for the year and the payment of our annual incentives. Free cash flow generation is expected to accelerate throughout the year, consistent with historical trends. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Great Start to the Year Anchored on a Very Solid Core </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Year over year,
our Core Divisions collectively grew by 34% and expanded operating margins by more than 300 bps. Each of the three Core Divisions delivered very strong growth and expanded margins&#151;driven by increased activity, pricing, and technology adoption.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;In our Core, we continue to leverage the industry&#146;s most comprehensive technology portfolio with disruptive <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">fit-for-basin</FONT></FONT> technologies, advanced digital solutions, and an unmatched ability to integrate across the entire value chain&#151;from subsurface to midstream. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;In our Digital&nbsp;&amp; Integration Division, digital sales posted strong
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> growth that is on track with our strategic ambition as we continue to secure new contracts and accelerate cloud and edge solutions. However, the increase in
digital sales during the quarter was largely offset by a decline in Asset Performance Solutions (APS) revenue, arising from production interruptions in Ecuador and lower revenue from our Palliser asset in Canada. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>A Resilient Cycle&#151;Powered by the International and Offshore Markets </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Looking at the macro, we maintain our very constructive multiyear outlook as the upcycle attributes and key activity drivers continue to evolve very positively.
The international and offshore markets continue to experience a strong resurgence of activity driven by resilient long-cycle development and capacity expansion projects. In contrast, the North American land market, which has led this upcycle in the
early innings, could potentially result in an activity plateau in 2023 due to lower gas prices and capital restraint by private E&amp;P operators. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;On
balance, the global activity outlook for the full year remains very solid. Through the first quarter, the resilience, breadth, and durability of this upcycle have become more evident, particularly in the international markets. These attributes are
highlighted by the following factors. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;First, there is broader recognition of the positive long-term demand outlook for oil and gas and the potential for a
stronger demand rebound in the second half of the year. In addition, recent OPEC+ decisions continue to keep commodity prices at supportive levels&#151;providing operators increased confidence to execute their projects. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Second, broad-based investments to expand oil capacity and diversify gas supply have been reinforced by the capex plans recently announced by major IOCs and NOCs.
Most of the announced budgets highlight a significant increase in spending that supports multiyear activity growth in key resource basins all over the world. In fact, we expect investments will become even more extensive internationally as the
pursuit of supply diversity remains a global priority and gathers greater urgency. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;And third, the durability of the current cycle is underscored by the
nature of the ongoing investments with the emergence of gas as a long-term energy transition fuel and enabler of energy security, the prominence of long-cycle projects, and the pivot to the Middle East and offshore basins as the anchors of supply
growth. Finally, the return of global exploration and appraisal will likely extend this cycle of investment for a number of years. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Taken together, these market dynamics play to our strengths and create an advantaged position for SLB. Our
strategy, global footprint, unique integration capabilities, and portfolio actions have strengthened our ability to support our customers. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Sequential Revenue
Growth and Margin Expansion Ahead</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;Looking ahead to the second quarter, we expect strong growth with seasonal recovery in the Northern Hemisphere, capacity
expansion projects in the Middle East that are in various stages of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ramp-up,</FONT> and robust activity in Asia and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Sahara</FONT> Africa. This growth scenario provides support for
broad sequential margin expansion across the Divisions and geographies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;I am excited about our start to the year, which gives us even further confidence in
our full-year 2023 and through-cycle targets. We are laser-focused on execution, supporting our customers, and delivering on our goals for the year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;I would
like to thank our team for delivering these strong results and performing for our customers and stakeholders.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Other Events </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">During the quarter, SLB repurchased approximately 4.4&nbsp;million shares of its common stock at an average price of $52.65 per share for a total purchase price of
$230&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">On February&nbsp;3, 2023, SLB completed the acquisition of Gyrodata Incorporated, a global company specializing in gyroscopic wellbore
positioning and survey technology. The transaction incorporates Gyrodata&#146;s wellbore placement and surveying technologies within SLB&#146;s Well Construction business, further enhancing its ability to deliver innovative drilling solutions to
customers. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">On April&nbsp;20, 2023, SLB&#146;s Board of Directors approved a quarterly cash dividend of $0.25 per share of outstanding common stock, payable on
July&nbsp;13, 2023, to stockholders of record on June&nbsp;7, 2023. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">4 </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">n/m = not meaningful </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>International </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Revenue in <B>Latin America</B> of $1.6&nbsp;billion increased 34% year on year due to robust drilling activity and improved pricing, higher sales of offshore production
systems in Brazil and Guyana, and increased stimulation work in Argentina. Sequentially, revenue was essentially flat as higher drilling activity was offset by reduced APS revenue in Ecuador due to production interruptions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Europe</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;&amp; Africa</B> revenue of $2.0&nbsp;billion grew 41% year on year primarily from higher sales of production systems in Europe and
Scandinavia and increased exploration and production activity offshore Africa. Sequentially, revenue decreased 5% primarily driven by Russia. Excluding Russia, revenue grew 2% sequentially due to higher drilling activity from new projects in Angola,
Gabon, and Namibia and increased sales of production systems in Europe. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Revenue in the <B>Middle East</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;&amp; Asia</B> of $2.4&nbsp;billion
increased 18% year on year due to higher drilling, intervention, and evaluation activity in Saudi Arabia, United Arab Emirates, Qatar, and Oman and across Southeast Asia and Australia. Sequentially, revenue decreased 5% due to seasonally lower
activity in Asia, weather-impacted stimulation activity in Saudi Arabia, and reduced sales of production systems across the area following the strong <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> sales in the previous quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>North America </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>North America</B> revenue of $1.7&nbsp;billion grew 32%
year on year due to strong land and offshore drilling and higher sales of production systems. US land revenue increased, driven by Well Construction revenue growth that outperformed the rig count growth, in addition to higher Production Systems
revenue. North America offshore revenue grew due to increases in drilling activity, exploration data licensing sales, and sales of subsea production systems in the US Gulf of Mexico. Sequentially, North America revenue increased 4% due to higher
land and offshore drilling and increased sales of subsea production systems, which were partially offset by lower APS revenue in Canada. Revenue from both Well Construction and Production Systems grew 9% sequentially. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">5 </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Digital&nbsp;&amp; Integration revenue of $894&nbsp;million increased 4% year on year as a result of continued growth in digital sales and increased exploration data
license sales in the US Gulf of Mexico, which were partially offset by lower revenue from APS projects. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sequentially, revenue declined 12% due to lower revenue
from APS projects and seasonally lower sales of digital and exploration data licenses following strong <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> sales. The APS revenue decline resulted primarily from a temporary production interruption in our
projects in Ecuador due to a pipeline disruption. Additionally, lower commodity prices impacted our project in Canada. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Digital&nbsp;&amp; Integration pretax
operating margin of 30% decreased 440 bps year on year as the continued growth in digital sales was more than offset by lower APS revenue. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sequentially, pretax
operating margin decreased eight percentage points due to seasonally lower sales of digital and exploration data licenses and lower APS revenue. Pretax operating margin is expected to expand next quarter on higher digital sales and increased revenue
from APS projects. </P>

Performance revenue of $1.5&nbsp;billion grew 24% year on year due to increased intervention, evaluation, and stimulation services across all areas on land and offshore and from both exploration and production activity. More than 30% revenue growth
was recorded both in Latin America, mainly from higher intervention activity, and in Europe&nbsp;&amp; Africa, largely from new evaluation and stimulation projects. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sequentially, revenue decreased 3% due to seasonal activity reductions in Europe and Asia, weather-impacted activity in the Middle East, and lower revenue in Russia.
These declines were partially offset by strong evaluation activity in Latin America, while North America revenue was essentially flat. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Reservoir Performance pretax
operating margin of 16% expanded 291 bps year on year with profitability improving across the international market driven by higher activity and improved pricing across evaluation, intervention, and stimulation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sequentially, pretax operating margin decreased 207 bps due to reduced profitability from the seasonal decline in stimulation activity internationally, primarily in the
Northern Hemisphere, which more than offset the strong margin expansion in North America. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Well Construction </B></P>

revenue of $3.3&nbsp;billion increased 36% year on year driven by strong activity and solid pricing improvements led by North America and Latin America, both of which grew more than 45%. Europe&nbsp;&amp; Africa revenue increased 38% while Middle
East&nbsp;&amp; Asia revenue grew 24% year on year. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">7 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">
Double-digit revenue growth was recorded both on land and offshore in fluids, measurements, integrated well construction, drilling, and equipment sales. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sequentially, revenue was slightly higher, driven by increased drilling, measurements, and integrated well construction activity, mainly on land and offshore North
America; in Latin America, primarily in Mexico and Brazil; and offshore Africa. These increases were partially offset by lower revenue in Russia and seasonal reductions in Asia. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Well Construction pretax operating margin of 21% expanded 444 bps year on year with profitability improving in measurements, integrated drilling, equipment sales, and
fluids across most areas driven by higher activity and improved pricing. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sequentially, pretax operating margin was essentially flat as improved profitability in
Latin America was offset by reduced margin in the Northern Hemisphere due to seasonality. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Production Systems </B></P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">n/m&nbsp; =&nbsp; not meaningful </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Production
Systems revenue of $2.2&nbsp;billion increased 38% year on year driven by strong activity across all areas led by Europe&nbsp;&amp; Africa and Latin America, which grew 63% and 50%, respectively. North America revenue increased 32% while Middle
East&nbsp;&amp; Asia revenue grew 11% year on year. Midstream, subsea, artificial lift sales, completions, and valves each recorded double-digit growth across North America and internationally. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sequentially, revenue was flat. Strong sales of subsea production systems offshore North America and Trinidad, higher sales of valves in US land, and robust sales of
midstream production systems in Europe were offset by lower revenue in the Middle East&nbsp;&amp; Asia and Russia following the strong <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> sales of the previous quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Production Systems pretax operating margin of 9% expanded 217 bps year on year mainly driven by higher artificial lift, surface, and subsea sales and execution
efficiency as supply chain and logistics constraints continued to ease. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sequentially, pretax operating margin contracted 148 bps as improved profitability from
increasing activity, coupled with execution efficiency in North America, was more than offset by reduced margins in Europe&nbsp;&amp; Africa and Asia due to seasonality and activity mix. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">During the quarter, SLB introduced the EcoShield<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&#153;</SUP> geopolymer
cement-free system that minimizes the CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2 </SUB>footprint of a well&#146;s construction. This innovative technology eliminates up to 85% of embodied
CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> emissions compared with conventional well cementing systems. The EcoShield system has the potential to avoid up to 5&nbsp;million metric tons of CO<SUB
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> emissions annually, the equivalent of removing 1.1&nbsp;million cars from the road each year. The EcoShield system uses locally sourced natural materials and industrial waste streams in its
composition, making it a far more sustainable well integrity method. The cement-free system can be deployed throughout various phases of the well life cycle, including abandonment, and across a range of field applications, including in corrosive
environments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Aker BP in Norway collaborated with SLB to deploy the Epilogue<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&#153;</SUP>
dual-string barrier evaluation on multiple wells to avoid excessive cement remediation. The results from the Epilogue dual-string barrier evaluation and a pressure test validated the presence of a barrier that complied with NORSOK regulations. The
Epilogue dual-string barrier evaluation eliminated the need for removing the production tubing before the bond evaluation, thereby saving rig time and providing operational flexibility. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">In Libya, SLB technology and processes enhanced production from the first six wells of a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">25-well</FONT> project for Sarir Oil Operations (SOO). The production enhancement workflow included project assessment, intelligent candidate selection, data processing, hypothesis validation, technology selection,
and production enhancement execution. An integrated suite of production logging and pulsed-neutron technologies was deployed to identify sources of water. High-resistance through-tubing bridge plugs and specialized ultra-shear cement were used to
shut off the water source in the high-pressure wells. The intervention campaign on these wells resulted in a 400% increase in oil production and reduction in water cut by 60%. The campaign allowed SOO to achieve its production increase objectives
and to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">de-bottleneck</FONT> produced water, thereby increasing overall field production. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

MaxFORTE<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&#153;</SUP> electric submersible pumps (ESPs) on their Orlando Field, North Sea, development well <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3/03b-13Y.</FONT> High-reliability and dual ESP completions
are key enablers of production assurance offshore, where workover costs are high and scheduling ESP replacements is limited by rig availability and weather windows in the North Sea. Following commissioning, the MaxFORTE high-reliability ESP system
operated at oil production rates greater than 4,000 barrels per day and continues its strong performance. This successful first application creates more opportunities for dual MaxFORTE ESP system installations offshore and subsea worldwide as
countries aim to align energy delivery with domestic needs.</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">CPC Corporation, Taiwan (CPC) has signed a global strategic cooperation framework agreement with SLB to collaborate on
digital transformation, including the deployment of a cloud-based cognitive E&amp;P platform; carbon capture, utilization, and sequestration (CCUS); and the assessment of geothermal prospects. These technologies align with Taiwan&#146;s drive
towards a 2050 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">net-zero</FONT> economy and CPC&#146;s actions in pivoting to a low carbon future. Leveraging the long-term cooperation between the two companies in oil and gas E&amp;P in Taiwan and elsewhere, the
expansion of the strategic cooperation will support CPC in accelerating its energy transition pathway. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">In Pakistan, Mari Petroleum Company Limited signed a contract with SLB for integrated digital drilling services to increase
their efficiency in the planning and execution of an upcoming strategic well. The contract will introduce the DrillPlan<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&#153;</SUP> coherent well construction planning solution and the DrillOps<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&#153;</SUP> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-target</FONT> well delivery solution. The SLB solutions will include integrated well planning, performance monitoring, and predictive analytics in the Delfi
digital platform. These SLB digital drilling solutions will enable agile decisions by both headquarters and wellsite operation teams. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">SLB and the national agency for the valorization of hydrocarbon resources in Algeria (ALNAFT) launched the EXplore ALgeria
Today (EXALT) upstream gateway, a fully integrated digital platform developed by SLB that enables seamless global access to a required portfolio of Algerian subsurface data and evergreening products. The multiyear agreement will be enabled by SLB
digital subsurface platform and domain expertise. A joint team of ALNAFT and SLB experts will upgrade subsurface understanding with new data to evaluate onshore and offshore hydrocarbon potential for new and existing operators.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">SLB has entered into a strategic partnership with Cognite to integrate the SLB Enterprise Data Solution for subsurface data
with Cognite Data Fusion<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>, Cognite&#146;s leading open industrial DataOps platform&#151;creating the first offering in the market with access to contextualized operational data in an
interoperable platform. Through this partnership, customers can integrate data from reservoirs, wells, and facilities in a single, open platform and leverage embedded AI and advanced analytics tools to optimize production and reduce costs, while
decreasing their operational footprint to help achieve sustainability goals. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>NEW ENERGY </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Customers are
increasingly focused on reducing their carbon equivalent emissions throughout the value chain. SLB is applying its scale and expertise to new energy systems, accelerating the path to net zero and beyond. Notable highlights include the following:
</P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">As part of Chevron Australia&#146;s commitment to exploring carbon capture and storage (CCS) potential in the Carnarvon
Basin, offshore Western Australia, SLB will perform a three-dimensional seismic and storage assessment to identify new CCS opportunities in the Barrow and Dampier <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-basins.</FONT> A global team of multidisciplinary
experts will integrate decades of subsurface knowledge to screen and evaluate potential CCS sites at the regional scale. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Also in Australia, SLB has supported Mitsui in its CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB>
sequestration assessment, which contemplates the injection of up to 50 metric tons of industry grade CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> into a depleted gas reservoir. SLB has successfully completed phase 1 of the project,
which involves flow assurance and engineering. Although detailed engineering for phases 2 and 3 is ongoing, the partners intend to proceed with the activity upon receipt of all necessary regulatory approvals. This will be the first CCS project on
land in the Perth Basin, and SLB will support Mitsui in executing the full CCS workflow, including flow assurance, CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> supply, injection system design, wellsite services, and third-party
project management. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Eni awarded SLB a contract to supply CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> injection trees and
wellheads for the HyNet Northwest CCS project. The contract includes 14 Cameron tubing spools and trees, three new Cameron wellheads, installation and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">plug-and-abandon</FONT></FONT>
services, and rental tooling. The HyNet project is a significant part of the UK government&#146;s strategy to achieve net zero by 2050. CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> emissions from the project will be stored for the
long term in a depleted field in the East Irish Sea through the repurposing of existing offshore infrastructure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">In Malaysia, SLB was awarded a contract by Malaysia Marine and Heavy Engineering Sdn Bhd, for work on the project of
PETRONAS, namely its Kasawari CCS project in Block SK316, offshore Sarawak. The scope of work is the design and supply of equipment to treat up to 256.3 MMscfd of inlet gas with 57.9 to 71.7 mol%
CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB>.The project is expected to reduce CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> emitted by flaring by 3.3 metric tons of
CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB><SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">e</SUB> annually, making it one of the largest offshore CCS projects in the world. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">In Canada, SLB is providing seismic processing and reservoir modeling software to support a shallow carbon storage project
for Carbon Management Canada&#146;s Newell County Facility. Research at the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">200-hectare</FONT> site demonstrates best practices for CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> storage monitoring
protocols and helps governments, industries, and the public understand that CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> can be stored securely underground. Access to seven years&#146; worth of operations research and data from the
project will enable SLB to validate its CO<SUB STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> monitoring, modeling, and imaging technologies, expanding its capabilities to deliver CCS solutions at scale. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">In upstate New York, United States, Cornell University awarded SLB a contract for integrated services to construct and
characterize a stratigraphic well on the university campus. The goal of the project is to evaluate the feasibility of sustainably heating the campus with Earth Source Heat. The well was successfully completed with several new technologies suited for
the stringent environmental and technical requirements of the project, including, among others, the DrillPlan well construction planning solution, DrillOps well delivery solution, HydraGlyde<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&#153;</SUP>
high-performance water-based drilling fluid, and MDT<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&#153;</SUP> modular formation dynamics tester deployed with a new 10K dual-packer system for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">state-of-the</FONT></FONT> art sampling and characterization. The well was drilled to the target zone with no fluid performance issues and was successfully tested and characterized as per project specifications. This
geothermal project is key to Cornell University&#146;s carbon neutrality goal by 2035. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(1)</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">&#147;Net Debt&#148; represents gross debt less cash and short-term investments. Management believes that Net Debt
provides useful information regarding the level of SLB&#146;s indebtedness by reflecting cash and investments that could be used to repay debt. Net Debt is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure that should be
considered in addition to, not as a substitute for or superior to, total debt. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(2)</SUP></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">See section entitled &#147;Charges&nbsp;&amp; Credits&#148; for details. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(3)</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes depreciation of fixed assets and amortization of intangible assets, exploration data costs, and APS investments.<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top"> </SUP> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(4)</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">&#147;Free cash flow&#148; represents cash flow from operations less capital expenditures, APS investments, and
exploration data costs capitalized. Management believes that free cash flow is an important liquidity measure for the company and that it is useful to investors and management as a measure of SLB&#146;s ability to generate cash. Once business needs
and obligations are met, this cash can be used to reinvest in the company for future growth or to return to shareholders through dividend payments or share repurchases. Free cash flow does not represent the residual cash flow available for
discretionary expenditures. Free cash flow is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure that should be considered in addition to, not as a substitute for or superior to, cash flow from operations. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">15 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Charges&nbsp;&amp; Credits </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">In addition to financial results determined in accordance with US generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP), this first-quarter 2023 earnings release also
includes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures (as defined under the SEC&#146;s Regulation G). In addition to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures discussed under
&#147;Liquidity&#148;, net income, excluding charges&nbsp;&amp; credits, as well as measures derived from it (including diluted EPS, excluding charges&nbsp;&amp; credits; SLB net income, excluding charges&nbsp;&amp; credits; effective tax rate,
excluding charges&nbsp;&amp; credits; and adjusted EBITDA) are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. Management believes that the exclusion of charges&nbsp;&amp; credits from these financial measures enables it to
evaluate more effectively SLB&#146;s operations period over period and to identify operating trends that could otherwise be masked by the excluded items. These measures are also used by management as performance measures in determining certain
incentive compensation. The foregoing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should be considered in addition to, not as a substitute for or superior to, other measures of financial performance prepared in accordance
with GAAP. The following is a reconciliation of certain of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures to the comparable GAAP measures. For a reconciliation of adjusted EBITDA to the comparable GAAP measure, please refer to the
section titled &#147;Supplementary Information&#148; (Question 9). </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Supplementary Information </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Frequently Asked Questions </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left"><B>What is the capital investment guidance for the full-year 2023? </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Capital investment (composed of capex, exploration data costs, and APS investments) for the full-year 2023 is still expected to be approximately $2.5 to
$2.6&nbsp;billion. Capital investment for the full-year 2022 was $2.3&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>2)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left"><B>What were cash flow from operations and free cash flow for the first quarter of 2023? </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Cash flow from operations for the first quarter of 2023 was $330&nbsp;million, and free cash flow was negative $265&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>3)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left"><B>What was included in &#147;Interest&nbsp;&amp; other income&#148; for the first quarter of 2023?

</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The difference consists of corporate items, charges and credits, and interest income and interest expense not allocated to the
segments as well as stock-based compensation expense, amortization expense associated with certain intangible assets, certain centrally managed initiatives, and other nonoperating items. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The ETR for the first quarter of 2023, calculated in accordance with GAAP, was 18.7% as compared to 19.6% for the fourth quarter of 2022. Excluding
charges and credits, the ETR for the first quarter of 2023 was 18.6% compared to 18.7% for the fourth quarter of 2022. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Adjusted EBITDA represents income before taxes, excluding charges&nbsp;&amp; credits, depreciation and amortization,
interest expense, and interest income. Management believes that adjusted EBITDA is an important profitability measure for SLB and that it allows investors and management to more efficiently evaluate SLB&#146;s operations period over period and to
identify operating trends that could otherwise be masked. Adjusted EBITDA is also used by management as a performance measure in determining certain incentive compensation. Adjusted EBITDA should be considered in addition to, not as a substitute for
or superior to, other measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left"><B>What does the pretax credit of $36&nbsp;million recorded during the first quarter of 2023 relate to?
</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">During the first quarter of 2023, SLB sold all of its remaining approximately 9&nbsp;million shares in Liberty and received
net proceeds of $137&nbsp;million. This gain is classified in <I>Interest</I><I></I><I>&nbsp;&amp; other income </I>in the <I>Consolidated Statement of Income</I>. As of March&nbsp;31, 2023, SLB no longer had an equity interest in Liberty. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About SLB </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">SLB (NYSE: SLB) is a global technology company driving energy
innovation for a balanced planet. With a global presence in more than 100 countries and employees representing almost twice as many nationalities, we work each day on innovating oil and gas, delivering digital at scale, decarbonizing industries, and
developing and scaling new energy systems that accelerate the energy transition. Find out more at slb.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Conference Call Information </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">SLB will hold a conference call to discuss the earnings press release and business outlook on Friday, April&nbsp;21, 2023. The call is scheduled to begin at 9:30 a.m. US
Eastern Time. To access the call, which is open to the public, please contact the conference call operator at +1 (844) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">721-7241</FONT> within North America, or +1 (409)
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">207-6955</FONT> outside North America, approximately 10 minutes prior to the call&#146;s scheduled start time, and provide the access code 8858313. At the conclusion of the conference call, an audio replay will be
